		name = komiintro.0.a
	}
}

country_event = { #Svetlana distinguishes herself as a valuable asset
	id = KOM.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM.1"}
	title = KOM.1.t
	desc = KOM.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalina_1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept her as an agent
		name = KOM.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = KOM.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { KOMStalinaInfluenceTemp = 3 }
        KOM_stalina_influence_change = yes
	}
	option = { #She cannot be trusted
		name = KOM.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = KOM.4
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Voz cuts ties
	id = KOM.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM.8"}
	title = KOM.8.t
	desc = KOM.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = KOM.8.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KOMZhdanovFavors > 15 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.9
					days = 2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KOMZhdanovFavors < 16 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.10
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KOM_VOZNESENSKY_CUT_TIES
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { KOMVoznesenskyInfluenceTemp = -5 }
	KOM_voznesensky_influence_change = yes
		}

		set_temp_variable = { KOMCenterPowerTemp = -1 }

				}

country_event = { #The election process begins - violence at the polls
	id = KOM.172
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM.172"}
	title = KOM.172.t
	desc = KOM.172.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_bobbies_riot

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap = KOMCenterPower }
		subtract_from_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap = KOMLeftPower }
		set_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap = KOMCenterPower }
		subtract_from_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap = KOMRightPower }
		set_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap = KOMLeftPower }
		subtract_from_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap = KOMRightPower }
	}

	option = {
		name = KOM.172.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { minorities_policy_monthly_change = 0 }
			KOM_elect_the_president = yes
			#Centrist majority government
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { KOMCenterPower > KOMLeftPower }
						check_variable = { KOMCenterPower > KOMRightPower }
						check_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap > 14 }
						check_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap > 14 }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.173
					days = 7
				}
			}
			#Leftist majority government
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { KOMLeftPower > KOMCenterPower }
						check_variable = { KOMLeftPower > KOMRightPower }
						check_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap < -14 }
						check_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap > 14 }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.174
					days = 7
				}
			}
			#Rightist majority government
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMCenterPower }
						check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMLeftPower }
						check_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap < -14 }
						check_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap < -14 }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.175
					days = 7
				}
			}
			#Centrist plurality government
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { KOMCenterPower > KOMLeftPower }
						check_variable = { KOMCenterPower > KOMRightPower }
						NOT = {
							check_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap < 15 }
							check_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap < 15 }
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.176
					days = 7
				}
			}
			#Leftist plurality government
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { KOMLeftPower > KOMCenterPower }
						check_variable = { KOMLeftPower > KOMRightPower }
						NOT = {
							check_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap < -14 }
							check_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap > 14 }
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.177
					days = 7
				}
			}
			#Rightist plurality government
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMCenterPower }
						check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMLeftPower }
						NOT = {
							check_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap < -14 }
							check_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap < -14 }
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.178
					days = 7
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = KOM_PRESIDENT_DEM
					}
					country_event = {
						id = KOM.176
						days = 7
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = KOM_PRESIDENT_COMMIE
					}
					country_event = {
						id = KOM.177
						days = 7
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = KOM_PRESIDENT_FASH
					}
					country_event = {
						id = KOM.178
						days = 7
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KOMLeftPower > KOMRightPower }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.179
					days = 7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMLeftPower }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.180
					days = 7
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						country_event = {
							id = KOM.179
							days = 7
						}
					}
					50 = {
						country_event = {
							id = KOM.180
							days = 7
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { KOMCoupRisk = 1 }
		set_country_flag = KOM_POST_ELECTION
	}

	id = KOM.248
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM.248"}
	title = KOM.248.t
	desc = KOM.248.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_komi_paramils_3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = KOM.248.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KOM_false_info
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.249
					hours = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KOM_true_info
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.250
					hours = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.251
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = KOM.278
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM.278"}
	title = KOM.278.t
	desc = KOM.278.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_komi_communist_party_headquarters

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ally with Suslov
		name = KOM.278.a
		set_temp_variable = { KOMBukharinaInfluenceTemp = 1 }
            KOM_bukharina_influence_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOMSuslovInfluenceTemp = 3 }
            KOM_suslov_influence_change = yes
	}
	option = { #Ally with Zhdanov
		name = KOM.278.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = KOM_Zhdanov_Dead
					has_country_flag = KOM_Zhdanov_Retired
					has_country_flag = KOM_Zhdanov_Arrested
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { KOMBukharinaInfluenceTemp = 1 }
            KOM_bukharina_influence_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOMZhdanovInfluenceTemp = 3 }
            KOM_zhdanov_influence_change = yes
	}
	option = { #Party unity be damned!
		name = KOM.278.c
		set_temp_variable = { KOMBukharinaInfluenceTemp = 5 }
            KOM_bukharina_influence_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOMLeftPowerTemp = -1 }
        KOM_left_power_change = yes
		KOM_increase_coup_risk_med = yes
	}
}

				check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMLeftPower }
			}
			KOM_decrease_coup_risk_low = yes
		}
		else = {
			KOM_increase_coup_risk_med = yes
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = komidiplo.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_government = socialist
						has_government = communist
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		KOM = {

				id = komidiplo.2
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}

			factor = 0
		}

	}

		}

			}
		}
	}

			popularity = 0.02
		}

				ideology = liberal_democracy
				popularity = 0.01
			}

				RUS_add_ruling_party_temp_pop_small = yes

			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Shafarevich meets with several figures from the Center and sweet-talks them into supporting mandating the KPK dissolve.
	id = komi_RNP.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event komi_RNP.3"}
	title = komi_RNP.3.t
	desc = komi_RNP.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_komi_bombing_2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = komi_RNP.3.a
		set_temp_variable = { KOMKosyginInfluenceTemp = 1 }
           KOM_kosygin_influence_change = yes
		add_political_power = -50
		country_event = {
			id = komi_RNP.4
			days = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = komi_RNP.7
				days = 20
				random = 240
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Suslov is tipped off and flees the country with most of his staff and associates.
	id = komi_RNP.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event komi_RNP.4"}
	title = komi_RNP.4.t
	desc = komi_RNP.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_komi_bombing_2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = komi_RNP.4.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = KOM_suslov_flee_tt
		set_country_flag = KOM_Suslov_Retired
		set_variable = { KOMSuslovInfluence = 0 }
		KOM_eliminate_left_leader = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = KOM_bukharina_flee_tt
		set_country_flag = KOM_Bukharina_Retired
		set_variable = { KOMBukharinaInfluence = 0 }
		hidden_effect = {
			KOM_eliminate_left_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = KOM_Bukharina_Dead
						has_country_flag = KOM_Bukharina_Arrested
						has_country_flag = KOM_Bukharina_Recovered
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					KOM_Power_Vacuum = {
						promote_character = { ideology = communist_subtype }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				KOM_Svetlana_Bukharina = {
					promote_character = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = KOM_Zhdanov_Dead
						has_country_flag = KOM_Zhdanov_Arrested
						has_country_flag = KOM_Zhdanov_Retired
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KOM_zhdanov_flee_tt
			set_country_flag = KOM_Zhdanov_Retired
			set_variable = { KOMZhdanovInfluence = 0 }
			hidden_effect = {
				KOM_eliminate_left_leader = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { KOMLeftPower = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}
